def twoSum(nums, target):
    p, q = 0, len(nums) - 1

    while p < q:
        v = nums[p] + nums[q]
        if v == traget:
            return p + 1, q+1
        
        # update pointer
        if v < target:
            p += 1
        else:
            q -= 1 ^PoK9SlbK
